12.6 Appendix 6 
Protocol: Purification of miRNA and mRNA from tissue (RNA later) using GentleMACS 
 
Kit: 
 
miRNeasy Mini Kit (Qiagen, # 217004) 
 
 
  
 
Homogenizer:  
GentleMACS + M tubes 
 
1. Place the centrifuge at 4°C. 
 
2. Remove DNase from freezer. 
 
3. Wash the working area with 0.5 % NaOH solution and find homogenizer, scalpel, weighing 
trays, tweezers, tips, and pipettes. 
 
4. Dilute RPE/RWT buffer with 96-100 % EtOH at first time use. 
 
5. Transfer 1 ml of QIAzol Lysis Reagent to the desired number of M tubes. 
 
6. Dissect approx. 30 mg tissue with scalpel (a small piece of about 3x3 mm), cut into smaller 
pieces and transfer to M tube with QIAzol Lysis Reagent. It is important that the tissue is 
placed on the edge of the orange blade to ensure sufficient homogenization. Scalpel and twee-
zers are washed with 0.5 % NaOH between each sample. 
 
7. The tissue is homogenized on program RNA_02.01 (fresh tissue). Leave tubes with homoge-
nate at room for 5 minutes (or until the other samples are finished). 
 
8. Add 200 μl of chloroform to each M tube, close the lid of the tube and shake vigorously for 15 
seconds. The tube is left at room temperature for 2-3 min. 
 
9. Transfer homogenate mix to a 1.5 ml tube (found in kit) and centrifuge at 12000 g/14000 rpm 
for 15 min at 4°C. Switch off the cooling function afterwards. 
 
10. The homogenate is now divided into 3 phases. From the top phase is taken approx. 300 μl 
(2x150 µl) for a 2 ml tube (found in kit). 450 μl (1:1.5) of 100 % ethanol is added in the tube. The 
homogenate is mixed with the pipette and the pipette tip is left in the tube to be reused in step 
11-12. 
 
11. Pipette up to 600 μl of sample into a RNeasy Mini Spin Column in a 1.5ml collection tube 
(found in kit). Close the lid and centrifuge at 8000 g/10000 rpm for 15 sec at room temp. Dis-
card the flow-through. 
 
12. Repeat step 11 with the rest of the sample (max 600 μl).  
 
13. Pipette 350 μl RWT buffer (check that buffer solute is not precipitated) to the column and cen-
trifuge at 8000 g/10000 rpm for 15 sec at room temp. Discard the flow-through. 
 
14. Mix DNase I incubation mix: per sample, mix 10 µl DNase I stock solution with 70 µl DNA Di-
gestion Buffer. E.g. for 12 samples, mix 120 µl DNase I stock solution with 840 µl DNA Diges-
tion Buffer. Mix gently with pipette. 
==PAGE:120==
Laura-Christine Astrupgaard (s193766) 
Master Thesis 
Investigation of Regulation of Gla Proteins during Atherosclerosis Development in The Obese Ossabaw Pig Model 
 
119 
  
15. Pipette 78 μl DNase I incubation mix directly onto the RNeasy silica gel membrane and place 
the column at room temperature for 15 min (minimum). 
 
16. Pipette 350 μl RWT buffer to the column and centrifuge at 8000 g/10000 rpm for 15 sec at room 
temp. Discard the flow-through. 
 
17. Add 500 μl of RPE buffer to the column and centrifuge at 8000 g/10000 rpm for 15 sec at room 
temp. Discard the flow-through. 
 
18. Add 500 μl of RPE buffer again to the column and centrifuge at 8000 g/10000 rpm for 2 min at 
room temp. Discard the flow-through. 
 
19. Transfer column to a new collection tube. Centrifuge at 8000 g/10000 rpm for 1 min to dry the 
column. 
 
20. To elute, transfer the column to a new 1.5 ml tube, then add 50 μl of RNase free water to the 
RNeasy silica gel membrane. Centrifuge at 8000 g/10000 rpm for 1 min at room temp. 
 
21. If you need more RNA then ad additional 50µl RNase free water to the column then the column 
is centrifuged at 8000 g/ 10000 rpm for 1 min at room temp. 
 
22. Placed at -80 °C for storage. 
 
 
==PAGE:121==
Laura-Christine Astrupgaard (s193766) 
Master Thesis 
Investigation of Regulation of Gla Proteins during Atherosclerosis Development in The Obese Ossabaw Pig Model 
 
120 
Protocol: Automated purification of Total RNA, including miRNA from Blood collected 
into PAXgene Blood RNA tubes  
Kit:                                            PAXgene Blood miRNA (Qiagen, cat# 763134)  
RNase-Free DNase Set (Qiagen, cat#79254)  
 
 
Unless indicated perform all steps at room temperature  
Equilibrate the PAXgene RNA tubes to room temperature. 
Dilute BM3 and BM4 with 100% EtOH, at first time use.  
 
1. Switch on the QIAcube Connect. 
2. Load the necessary reagents and plastic ware into QIAcube. To save time this can be done 
during the following 10-minute centrifugation steps.  
a. Carefully fill the 4 reagent bottles listed up to the maximum indicator level or if that 
is not possible, to the level allowed by the buffer supplied in the kit. Note: Be sure 
to remove lids from the bottles before placing the bottle rack onto the workta-
ble.  
b. Place 2 tip racks filled with Filter-Tips 1000 μl. 
c. Label eppendorf tubes for each sample (1-12). 
d. Open the PAXgene Shredder spin columns to be used and cut the lids off completely 
using scissors. 
e. Load spin column, shredder spin column (without lid) and Eppendorf tubes in each 
labeled rotor adapter. Note: Make sure the lids in the slots of the rotor adapter 
can move.   
f. Load the assembled rotor adapters into the centrifuge buckets.  
3. Centrifuge the PAXgene Blood RNA Tube for 10 min at 3000g using a swing-out rotor (for 
round-bottom tubes.). 
4. Remove the supernatant by flipping the tube. Add 4 ml RNase-free water (with the auto-
matic pipette) to the pellet and close the tube using a fresh secondary Hemogard closure 
(provided in the kit).  
5. Vortex until the pellet is visibly dissolved, and centrifuge for 10 min at 3000 g. Remove the 
entire supernatant by flipping the tube and discard it.  
NOTE: Small debris remaining in the supernatant after vortexing but before centrifugation 
will not affect the procedure. Incomplete removal of the supernatant will inhibit lysis and 
dilute the lysate, affecting the conditions for binding RNA to the PAXgene membrane. 
6. Add 350 µl Buffer BM1, and vortex until the pellet is visibly dissolved.  
7. Pipet the sample into a 2 ml processing tube.  
8. Fill 3 processing tubes with proteinase K (kit box), DNase I incubation mix (DNase aliquots 
in freezer plus RDD buffer in the fridge) and buffer BR5. Label the tubes and place them 
into the appropriate position inside QIAcube. 
9. Load the tubes containing the sample into the shaker. The sample positions are numbered 
for ease of loading. Insert shaker racks plugs into the slots at the edge of the shaker rack 
next to each processing tube. This enables detection of samples during the load check. 
NOTE: Make sure that the correct Shaker Adapter (marked with a “2”) is installed. 
10. Close the hood and select part A of the protocol and start it.  
==PAGE:122==
Laura-Christine Astrupgaard (s193766) 
Master Thesis 
Investigation of Regulation of Gla Proteins during Atherosclerosis Development in The Obese Ossabaw Pig Model 
 
121 
Note: The QIAcube Connect will perform load checks for samples, tips, rotor adapters, and 
reagent bottles. 
11. Once is finished open the hood and remove and discard the spin columns from the rotor 
adapters and the empty processing tubes from the shaker.  
12. Close the lids of all 1.5 ml eppendorf tubes containing the purified RNA in the rotor adapt-
ers and transfer it onto the QIAcube Connect shaker adapter. 
13. Close the hood and select part B of the protocol and start it (denaturation step at 65C). 
14. Once finished place the tubes with purified RNA on ice and measure nanodrop. Then store 
at -80C.  
 
 
 
==PAGE:123==
Laura-Christine Astrupgaard (s193766) 
Master Thesis 
Investigation of Regulation of Gla Proteins during Atherosclerosis Development in The Obese Ossabaw Pig Model 
 
122 
Measurement of RNA integrity  
 
Needed: 
Agilent RNA 6000 Nano Kit 
RNase-free water 
 
 
Micro centrifuge 
Heating block for ladder/sample denaturation 
Program: 2100 expert Eukaryote Total RNA Nano 
 
1. Gel, dye, and marker must equilibrate for 30 min to room temperature before use. Protect 
dye and dye mixtures from light.  
2. If necessary, prepare dilutions of RNA in RNase-free water to approx. 100 ng/µl.  
3. Vortex RNA 6000 Nano dye and add 1μl of dye into a 65μl aliquot of filtered gel – this is 
sufficient for two chips. 
4. Vortex the gel-dye mix and centrifuge for 10 min at 13.000 x g (room temperature). Make 
sure lid points upwards. 
5. Samples (100 ng/µl, min. 3 µl) are heated for 2 min at 70 °C. Place on ice until use. If the 
ladder is being used for the first time, then heat the entire ladder along with the samples – 
otherwise just thaw it and keep it on ice. 
6. Place a RNA 6000 Nano chip in the priming station (setting C). Make sure the plunger is set 
at 1 ml. 
7. Add 9µl gel-dye to the black G well. 
 
 
 
 
8. Close the priming station and press the plunger to just below the clip. Leave for 30 seconds 
and release the plunger by pulling the handle. Let the plunger rise by itself for 5 seconds 
and the pull it all the way up to 1 ml again. Open the priming station. 
9. Add 9µl gel-dye to the other two G wells. 
 
 
 
 
10. Add 5 µl RNA 6000 Nano Marker to all sample and ladder wells. Add 6 µl if a well is to be 
left empty. 
 
 
 
 
11. Add 1 µl RNA 6000 Ladder to the ladder well and 1 µl sample to each sample well. 
==PAGE:124==
Laura-Christine Astrupgaard (s193766) 
Master Thesis 
Investigation of Regulation of Gla Proteins during Atherosclerosis Development in The Obese Ossabaw Pig Model 
 
123 
 
 
 
 
12. Shake chip in chip vortex for 1 min. 
13. Add 350µl RNase-free water to a random well in the clear cleaning chip and rinse the elec-
trodes for 10 seconds followed by air-drying for 10 seconds. 
14. Place chip in the Bioanalyzer, select the appropriate program (the one that fits the chip 
type), and start analysis. 
15. Enter sample names. 
Decontaminating the Electrodes 
To avoid decomposition of your RNA sample, follow this electrode decontamination procedure on a 
daily basis before running any RNA Nano assays. 
1. Slowly fill one of the wells of an electrode cleaner with 350 µl RNaseZAP.  
2. Open the lid and place electrode cleaner in the Agilent 2100 Bioanalyzer.  
3. Close the lid and leave it closed for about 1 minute.  
4. Open the lid and remove the electrode cleaner. Label the electrode cleaner and keep it for 
future use. You can reuse the electrode cleaner for all 25 chips in the kit.  
5. Slowly fill one of the wells of another electrode cleaner with 350µl RNase- free water. 
6. Place electrode cleaner in the Agilent 2100 Bioanalyzer.  
7. Close the lid and leave it closed for about 10 seconds.  
8. Open the lid and remove the electrode cleaner. Label it and keep it for further use.  
9. Wait another 10 seconds for the water on the electrodes to evaporate before closing the lid. 
 
Cleaning after a RNA 6000 Nano Chip Run 
1. Slowly fill one of the wells of the electrode cleaner with 350µl RNase- free water.  
2. Open the lid and place the electrode cleaner in the Agilent 2100 Bioanalyzer.  
3. Close the lid and leave it closed for about 10 seconds.   
4. Open the lid and remove the electrode cleaner.  
5. Wait another 10 seconds to allow the water on the electrodes to evaporate before closing 
the lid. 
After 5 chip runs, empty and refill the electrode cleaner.  
After 25 chip runs, replace the used electrode cleaner by a new one. 
 
Preparing the Gel (making aliquots) 
1. Allow all reagents to equilibrate to room temperature for 30 minutes before use. 
2. Place 550 µl of Agilent RNA 6000 Nano gel matrix (red  ) into the top receptacle of a spin 
filter. 
3. Place the spin filter in a micro centrifuge and spin for 10 minutes at 
1500 g ± 20 % (for Eppendorf micro centrifuge, this corresponds to 4000 rpm). 
==PAGE:125==
Laura-Christine Astrupgaard (s193766) 
Master Thesis 
Investigation of Regulation of Gla Proteins during Atherosclerosis Development in The Obese Ossabaw Pig Model 
 
124 
4. Aliquot 65 µl filtered gel into 0.5 ml RNase- free microfuge tubes that are included in the kit. 
Store the aliquots at 4 °C and use them within one month. 
 
For proper handling of the ladder (order no.: 5067-1529), following steps are necessary: 
1.  After reagent kit arrival, pipette the ladder in RNase- free vial.  
2. Heat denature it for 2 min at 70 °C. 
3.  Immediately cool down the vial on ice. 
4.  Prepare aliquots in RNase- free vials with the required amount for a typical 
daily use. 
5.  Store aliquots at - 70°C. 
6.  Before use, thaw ladder aliquots and keep them on ice (avoid extensive 
warming upon thawing process).
